### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/proposal.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 00:37:05
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/proposal.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/proposal.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Why
2: 
3: Currently, all projects clone from the default branch of the remote repository. Users need the ability to:
4: 1. Start from a specific branch (e.g., `feature/v2` instead of `main`)
5: 2. Create a dedicated branch for AI sessions (e.g., `ai-session-feature-x`)
6: 
7: This enables workflows where Mimo projects can work on feature branches or create isolated branches for AI-driven development without polluting the main branch.
8: 
9: ## What Changes
10: 
11: - Add `sourceBranch` field (optional) - specifies which branch to clone from; empty means use repository default
12: - Add `newBranch` field (optional) - creates and switches to a new branch locally after cloning
13: - Update project creation form with two new optional text fields
14: - Extend VCS layer to support cloning specific branches and creating new branches
15: - Modify session initialization to create new branch if specified
16: - Branch information is immutable after project creation
17: - No immediate push - branch gets pushed on first Commit action
18: 
19: ## Capabilities
20: 
21: ### New Capabilities
22: 
23: ### Modified Capabilities
24: - `projects`: Extend project creation to support branch selection and branch creation
25: - `vcs`: Add methods for cloning specific branches and creating new branches in both Git and Fossil
26: 
27: ## Impact
28: 
29: - **Database Schema**: Projects table gains `sourceBranch` and `newBranch` columns
30: - **VCS Layer**: New methods in `src/vcs/index.ts` for branch operations
31: - **UI**: Project creation form gets two new optional fields
32: - **Session Setup**: Branch creation logic added to session initialization
33: - **API**: No breaking changes - new fields are optional

(End of file - total 33 lines)
</content>
```


### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/design.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 00:37:05
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/design.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/design.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Context
2: 
3: Currently, projects are created by cloning the default branch from a remote repository. The VCS layer in `src/vcs/index.ts` supports cloning but doesn't handle branch selection. The session creation process in `src/sessions/routes.tsx` handles repository setup but assumes default branch behavior.
4: 
5: The Project model stores repository information but lacks branch-related fields. The UI forms for project creation need to collect optional branch preferences from users.
6: 
7: ## Goals / Non-Goals
8: 
9: **Goals:**
10: - Allow users to optionally specify a source branch to clone from (empty = repo default)
11: - Allow users to optionally create a new branch locally for the project
12: - Support both Git and Fossil VCS systems with their respective branch semantics
13: - Create branches during project initialization, not pushed immediately
14: - Branch info is immutable after project creation
15: 
16: **Non-Goals:**
17: - Branch validation against remote (user provides exact branch names)
18: - Immediate push of new branch (handled by existing Commit action)
19: - Editable branch settings after project creation
20: - Branch protection or permission checks
21: 
22: ## Decisions
23: 
24: ### 1. Branch Creation Timing
25: **Decision**: Create branch during session initialization, not during project creation.
26: **Rationale**: Project creation only stores metadata; actual repository clone happens when first session is created. This keeps project creation lightweight.
27: 
28: ### 2. No Branch Validation
29: **Decision**: Do not validate branch existence before cloning.
30: **Rationale**: Let the underlying VCS commands fail naturally if branch doesn't exist. This matches current behavior with repo URLs.
31: 
32: ### 3. Git vs Fossil Handling
33: **Decision**: Handle branch operations differently for each VCS:
34: - Git: Use `--branch` flag for clone, `checkout -b` for new branch
35: - Fossil: Clone full repo, then `checkout` for source branch, `branch new` for new branch
36: **Rationale**: Fossil has different branching model - all branches exist in the repo.
37: 
38: ### 4. Force Behavior
39: **Decision**: For Git, if new branch exists locally, overwrite. For Fossil, branch creation updates if exists.
40: **Rationale**: User wants to use this branch; if it exists, they want to work on it.
41: 
42: ## Risks / Trade-offs
43: 
44: - **Risk**: Invalid branch names cause clone failures
45:   - **Mitigation**: User sees VCS error message; can recreate project with correct name
46: 
47: - **Risk**: Branch name collisions if multiple projects use same newBranch name
48:   - **Mitigation**: Each project has isolated upstream directory; branches don't conflict
49: 
50: - **Risk**: Fossil `branch new` behavior differs from Git
51:   - **Mitigation**: Document behavior differences; Fossil updates existing branches gracefully
52: 
53: - **Trade-off**: No remote validation means user might typo branch name
54:   - **Acceptance**: Consistent with current URL behavior (we don't validate URLs exist)

(End of file - total 54 lines)
</content>
```

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/specs/projects/spec.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 00:37:08
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/specs/projects/spec.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-branch-selection/specs/projects/spec.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: Projects can specify source branch
4: The system SHALL allow projects to optionally specify a source branch to clone from. If not specified, the system SHALL use the repository's default branch.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create project with source branch
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user creates project with repoUrl "https://github.com/user/repo.git" and sourceBranch "feature/v2"
8: - **THEN** system stores project with sourceBranch "feature/v2"
9: - **AND** system clones from "feature/v2" branch when creating sessions
10: 
11: #### Scenario: Create project without source branch
12: - **WHEN** authenticated user creates project with repoUrl "https://github.com/user/repo.git" and no sourceBranch
13: - **THEN** system stores project without sourceBranch
14: - **AND** system clones from repository default branch when creating sessions
15: 
16: #### Scenario: Source branch field is optional
17: - **WHEN** authenticated user views project creation form
18: - **THEN** sourceBranch field is displayed as optional
19: - **AND** field help text indicates "Leave empty to use repository default branch"
20: 
21: ### Requirement: Projects can specify new branch
22: The system SHALL allow projects to optionally specify a new branch to create locally. The branch SHALL be created during session initialization.
23: 
24: #### Scenario: Create project with new branch
25: - **WHEN** authenticated user creates project with newBranch "ai-session-feature-x"
26: - **THEN** system stores project with newBranch "ai-session-feature-x"
27: - **AND** system creates branch locally after cloning
28: - **AND** system switches to new branch in upstream directory
29: 
30: #### Scenario: Create project with source and new branch
31: - **WHEN** authenticated user creates project with sourceBranch "develop" and newBranch "ai-feature"
32: - **THEN** system clones from "develop" branch
33: - **AND** system creates and switches to "ai-feature" branch
34: - **AND** new branch is based on "develop"
35: 
36: #### Scenario: New branch field is optional
37: - **WHEN** authenticated user views project creation form
38: - **THEN** newBranch field is displayed as optional
39: - **AND** field help text indicates "Create a dedicated branch for AI sessions"
40: 
41: ### Requirement: Branch information is immutable
42: The system SHALL store branch information immutably. Branch settings SHALL NOT be editable after project creation.
43: 
44: #### Scenario: View project with branches configured
45: - **WHEN** authenticated user views project detail with sourceBranch and newBranch configured
46: - **THEN** system displays sourceBranch and newBranch information
47: - **AND** system does not provide edit controls for branch fields
48: 
49: #### Scenario: Edit project form excludes branch fields
50: - **WHEN** authenticated user views project edit form
51: - **THEN** sourceBranch and newBranch fields are not displayed
52: - **AND** existing branch configuration remains unchanged
53: 
54: ### Requirement: Branch creation for Git repositories
55: The system SHALL create branches in Git repositories using git commands.
56: 
57: #### Scenario: Create Git branch
58: - **WHEN** project has repoType "git" and newBranch "feature-x"
59: - **AND** system initializes session
60: - **THEN** system executes "git checkout -b feature-x" in upstream directory
61: - **AND** if branch exists, system overwrites with new branch
62: 
63: #### Scenario: Clone Git with source branch
64: - **WHEN** project has repoType "git" and sourceBranch "develop"
65: - **AND** system initializes session
66: - **THEN** system executes "git clone --branch develop <repoUrl>"
67: 
68: ### Requirement: Branch creation for Fossil repositories
69: The system SHALL create branches in Fossil repositories using fossil commands.
70: 
71: #### Scenario: Create Fossil branch
72: - **WHEN** project has repoType "fossil" and newBranch "feature-x"
73: - **AND** system initializes session
74: - **THEN** system executes "fossil branch new feature-x current"
75: - **AND** if branch exists, fossil updates the branch pointer
76: 
77: #### Scenario: Checkout Fossil with source branch
78: - **WHEN** project has repoType "fossil" and sourceBranch "develop"
79: - **AND** system initializes session
80: - **THEN** system executes "fossil checkout develop" after opening repository
81: 
82: ### Requirement: No immediate push for new branches
83: The system SHALL NOT push new branches to remote during session initialization. Branch SHALL be pushed on first Commit action.
84: 
85: #### Scenario: New branch not pushed immediately
86: - **WHEN** project has newBranch "ai-session-1"
87: - **AND** system completes session initialization
88: - **THEN** new branch exists only locally in upstream directory
89: - **AND** no push command is executed
90: 
91: #### Scenario: New branch pushed on commit
92: - **WHEN** user clicks Commit button for session
93: - **AND** commit succeeds
94: - **THEN** push command includes the new branch
95: - **AND** branch appears in remote repository

(End of file - total 95 lines)
</content>
```


### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/projects/repository.ts

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 00:37:08
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/projects/repository.ts

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/projects/repository.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import { join } from "path";
2: import { existsSync, mkdirSync, writeFileSync, readFileSync, readdirSync, rmdirSync, unlinkSync } from "fs";
3: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
4: import { dump, load } from "js-yaml";
5: import crypto from "crypto";
6: 
7: export interface Project {
8:   id: string;
9:   name: string;
10:   repoUrl: string;
11:   repoType: "git" | "fossil";
12:   owner: string;
13:   createdAt: Date;
14:   description?: string;
15:   credentialId?: string;
16:   sourceBranch?: string;
17:   newBranch?: string;
18: }
19: 
20: export interface PublicProject {
21:   id: string;
22:   name: string;
23:   description?: string;
24:   repoType: "git" | "fossil";
25:   owner: string;
26:   createdAt: string;
27:   sourceBranch?: string;
28:   newBranch?: string;
29: }
30: 
31: export interface ProjectData {
32:   id: string;
33:   name: string;
34:   repoUrl: string;
35:   repoType: "git" | "fossil";
36:   owner: string;
37:   createdAt: string;
38:   description?: string;
39:   credentialId?: string;
40:   sourceBranch?: string;
41:   newBranch?: string;
42: }
43: 
44: export interface CreateProjectInput {
45:   name: string;
46:   repoUrl: string;
47:   repoType: "git" | "fossil";
48:   owner: string;
49:   description?: string;
50:   credentialId?: string;
51:   sourceBranch?: string;
52:   newBranch?: string;
53: }
54: 
55: export class ProjectRepository {
56:   private getProjectPath(id: string): string {
57:     return join(getPaths().projects, id);
58:   }
59: 
60:   private getProjectFilePath(id: string): string {
61:     return join(this.getProjectPath(id), "project.yaml");
62:   }
63: 
64:   private generateId(): string {
65:     return crypto.randomUUID();
66:   }
67: 
68:   async create(input: CreateProjectInput): Promise<Project> {
69:     if (input.description && input.description.length > 500) {
70:       throw new Error("Description must be 500 characters or less");
71:     }
72: 
73:     const id = this.generateId();
74:     const projectPath = this.getProjectPath(id);
75:     
76:     if (!existsSync(projectPath)) {
77:       mkdirSync(projectPath, { recursive: true });
78:     }
79: 
80:     const projectData: ProjectData = {
81:       id,
82:       name: input.name,
83:       repoUrl: input.repoUrl,
84:       repoType: input.repoType,
85:       owner: input.owner,
86:       createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
87:       ...(input.description && { description: input.description }),
88:       ...(input.credentialId && { credentialId: input.credentialId }),
89:       ...(input.sourceBranch && { sourceBranch: input.sourceBranch }),
90:       ...(input.newBranch && { newBranch: input.newBranch }),
91:     };
92: 
93:     writeFileSync(
94:       this.getProjectFilePath(id),
95:       dump(projectData),
96:       "utf-8"
97:     );
98: 
99:     return {
100:       ...projectData,
101:       createdAt: new Date(projectData.createdAt),
102:     };
103:   }
104: 
105:   async findById(id: string): Promise<Project | null> {
106:     const filePath = this.getProjectFilePath(id);
107:     if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
108:       return null;
109:     }
110: 
111:     const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
112:     const data = load(content) as ProjectData;
113:     
114:     return {
115:       ...data,
116:       createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
117:     };
118:   }
119: 
120:   async listByOwner(owner: string): Promise<Project[]> {
121:     const Paths = getPaths();
122:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
123:       return [];
124:     }
125: 
126:     const entries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
127:     const projects: Project[] = [];
128: 
129:     for (const entry of entries) {
130:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
131:         const projectFile = join(Paths.projects, entry.name, "project.yaml");
132:         if (existsSync(projectFile)) {
133:           const content = readFileSync(projectFile, "utf-8");
134:           const data = load(content) as ProjectData;
135:           if (data.owner === owner) {
136:             projects.push({
137:               ...data,
138:               createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
139:             });
140:           }
141:         }
142:       }
143:     }
144: 
145:     return projects;
146:   }

186:   async delete(id: string): Promise<void> {
187:     const projectPath = this.getProjectPath(id);
188:     
189:     if (existsSync(projectPath)) {
190:       // Delete project.yaml first
191:       const projectFile = this.getProjectFilePath(id);
192:       if (existsSync(projectFile)) {
193:         unlinkSync(projectFile);
194:       }
195:       
196:       // Delete any other files in the directory
197:       const entries = readdirSync(projectPath);
198:       for (const entry of entries) {
199:         const entryPath = join(projectPath, entry);
200:         if (existsSync(entryPath)) {
201:           unlinkSync(entryPath);
202:         }
203:       }
204:       
205:       // Delete the directory
206:       rmdirSync(projectPath);
207:     }
208:   }

210:   async exists(id: string): Promise<boolean> {
211:     return existsSync(this.getProjectFilePath(id));
212:   }

214:   async update(id: string, updates: { name?: string; repoUrl?: string; repoType?: "git" | "fossil"; description?: string; credentialId?: string }): Promise<Project> {
215:     const project = await this.findById(id);
216:     if (!project) {
217:       throw new Error("Project not found");
218:     }
219: 
220:     if (updates.description && updates.description.length > 500) {
221:       throw new Error("Description must be 500 characters or less");
222:     }
223: 
224:     const updatedData: ProjectData = {
225:       id: project.id,
226:       name: updates.name || project.name,
227:       repoUrl: updates.repoUrl || project.repoUrl,
228:       repoType: updates.repoType || project.repoType,
229:       owner: project.owner,
230:       createdAt: project.createdAt.toISOString(),
231:       description: updates.description,
232:       sourceBranch: project.sourceBranch,
233:       newBranch: project.newBranch,
234:     };
235: 
236:     // Handle credentialId specially - if undefined, keep existing; if null, remove; if string, set
237:     if ("credentialId" in updates) {
238:       if (updates.credentialId !== undefined) {
239:         updatedData.credentialId = updates.credentialId;
240:       }
241:     } else if (project.credentialId) {
242:       updatedData.credentialId = project.credentialId;
243:     }
244: 
245:     writeFileSync(
246:       this.getProjectFilePath(id),
247:       dump(updatedData),
248:       "utf-8"
249:     );
250: 
251:     return {
252:       ...updatedData,
253:       createdAt: new Date(updatedData.createdAt),
254:     };
```

```
14:   private async execCommand(
15:     command: string[],
16:     cwd?: string,
17:     env?: Record<string, string>
18:   ): Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }> {
19:     const proc = Bun.spawn(command, {
20:       cwd,
21:       stdout: "pipe",
22:       stderr: "pipe",
23:       env: env ? { ...process.env, ...env } : undefined,
24:     });
25: 
26:     const exitCode = await proc.exited;
27:     const stdout = await new Response(proc.stdout).text();
28:     const stderr = await new Response(proc.stderr).text();
29: 
30:     return {
31:       success: exitCode === 0,
32:       output: stdout.trim(),
33:       error: stderr.trim(),
34:     };
35:   }
36: 
37:   // Helper to inject HTTPS credentials into URL
38:   private injectHttpsCredentials(repoUrl: string, credential: Extract<Credential, { type: "https" }>): string {
39:     try {
40:       const url = new URL(repoUrl);
41:       url.username = encodeURIComponent(credential.username);
42:       url.password = encodeURIComponent(credential.password);
43:       return url.toString();
44:     } catch {
45:       // If URL parsing fails, assume it's SSH format and return as-is
46:       return repoUrl;
47:     }
48:   }
49: 
50:   // Helper to create temporary SSH key file
51:   private createTempSshKeyFile(privateKey: string): string {
52:     const tempDir = tmpdir();
53:     const keyFile = join(tempDir, `mimo-ssh-key-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2)}`);
54:     writeFileSync(keyFile, privateKey, { mode: 0o600 });
55:     chmodSync(keyFile, 0o600);
56:     return keyFile;
57:   }
58: 
59:   // Helper to delete temporary SSH key file
60:   private deleteTempSshKeyFile(keyPath: string): void {
61:     try {
62:       unlinkSync(keyPath);
63:     } catch {
64:       // Ignore errors during cleanup
65:     }
66:   }
67: 
68:   // Helper to build SSH command for GIT_SSH_COMMAND
69:   private buildGitSshCommand(keyPath: string): string {
70:     return `ssh -i "${keyPath}" -o IdentitiesOnly=yes -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o UserKnownHostsFile=/dev/null`;
71:   }
72: 
73:   // Helper to detect if URL is SSH
74:   private isSshUrl(url: string): boolean {
75:     return url.startsWith("git@") || url.startsWith("ssh://");
76:   }
77: 
78:   // Helper to check if error is authentication-related
79:   private isAuthError(error: string, type: "https" | "ssh"): boolean {
80:     const lowerError = error.toLowerCase();
81:     
82:     // Exclude network errors first
83:     if (lowerError.includes("timeout") || 
84:         lowerError.includes("could not resolve") ||
85:         lowerError.includes("network is unreachable") ||
86:         lowerError.includes("no route to host")) {
87:       return false;
88:     }
89:     
90:     if (type === "https") {
91:       return lowerError.includes("authentication failed") ||
92:              lowerError.includes("403") ||
93:              lowerError.includes("401") ||
94:              lowerError.includes("unauthorized");
95:     } else {
96:       return lowerError.includes("permission denied") ||
97:              lowerError.includes("publickey") ||
98:              lowerError.includes("authentication") ||
99:              lowerError.includes("host key verification failed");
100:     }
101:   }
102: 
103:   // Helper to safely move files across filesystems (handles EXDEV error)
104:   // When rename fails due to cross-device link, falls back to copy+delete
105:   private async safeMove(sourcePath: string, destPath: string, isDirectory: boolean): Promise<void> {
106:     const { renameSync, cpSync, rmSync, mkdirSync, existsSync, readdirSync } = await import("fs");
107:     const { dirname, join } = await import("path");
108: 
109:     try {
110:       // Try rename first (fastest for same filesystem)
111:       renameSync(sourcePath, destPath);
112:     } catch (error: any) {
113:       // If error is cross-device link, fall back to copy+delete
114:       if (error.code === "EXDEV" || error.message?.includes("cross-device")) {
115:         // Ensure parent directory exists for destination
116:         const parentDir = dirname(destPath);
117:         mkdirSync(parentDir, { recursive: true });
118:         
119:         if (isDirectory) {
120:           // Use cpSync with recursive and preserveTimestamps to properly copy .git
121:           cpSync(sourcePath, destPath, { 
122:             recursive: true, 
123:             preserveTimestamps: true,
124:             filter: () => true // Copy all files including hidden ones
125:           });
126:           // Verify copy succeeded before deleting source
127:           if (!existsSync(destPath)) {
128:             throw new Error(`Failed to copy directory from ${sourcePath} to ${destPath}`);
129:           }
130:           // Delete source directory recursively
131:           rmSync(sourcePath, { recursive: true, force: true });
132:         } else {
133:           // Use cpSync for files too to preserve permissions
134:           cpSync(sourcePath, destPath, { preserveTimestamps: true });
135:           if (!existsSync(destPath)) {
136:             throw new Error(`Failed to copy file from ${sourcePath} to ${destPath}`);
137:           }
138:           rmSync(sourcePath, { force: true });
139:         }
140:       } else {
141:         // Re-throw other errors
142:         throw error;
143:       }
144:     }
145:   }

249:   async importGitToFossil(gitUrl: string, workDir: string, credential?: Credential): Promise<VCSResult> {

251:     
252:     // Inject credentials if provided and HTTPS
253:     if (credential?.type === "https" && !this.isSshUrl(gitUrl)) {
254:       url = this.injectHttpsCredentials(gitUrl, credential);
255:     }
256: 
257:     try {
258:       new URL(url);
259:     } catch {

385:   async cloneRepository(
386:     repoUrl: string,
387:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
388:     targetDir: string,
389:     credential?: Credential,
390:     sourceBranch?: string
391:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
392:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
393:     
394:     // Ensure target directory exists
395:     try {
396:       mkdirSync(targetDir, { recursive: true });
397:     } catch {
398:       // Directory might already exist
399:     }
400: 
401:     if (repoType === "git") {
402:       let url = repoUrl;
403:       let sshKeyPath: string | null = null;
404:       let env: Record<string, string> | undefined = undefined;
405: 
406:       // Handle credentials
407:       if (credential) {
408:         if (credential.type === "https" && !this.isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
409:           url = this.injectHttpsCredentials(repoUrl, credential);
410:         } else if (credential.type === "ssh" && this.isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
411:           // Create temp SSH key file
412:           sshKeyPath = this.createTempSshKeyFile(credential.privateKey);
413:           env = {
414:             GIT_SSH_COMMAND: this.buildGitSshCommand(sshKeyPath),
415:           };
416:         }
417:       }
418: 
419:       try {
420:         // Clone Git repository with optional branch
421:         const cloneArgs = sourceBranch 
422:           ? ["git", "clone", "--branch", sourceBranch, url, targetDir]
423:           : ["git", "clone", url, targetDir];
424:         const result = await this.execCommand(
425:           cloneArgs,
426:           targetDir,
427:           env
428:         );
429:         
430:         if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, credential?.type === "ssh" ? "ssh" : "https")) {
431:           return {
432:             success: false,
433:             output: result.output,
434:             error: credential?.type === "ssh" 
435:               ? "SSH authentication failed. Please check your private key and repository access."
436:               : "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
437:           };
438:         }
439:         
440:         if (result.success) {
441:           return {
442:             success: true,
443:             output: result.output,
444:           };
445:         }
446:         
447:         // If git clone failed but directory has content, try cloning into current directory
448:         const result2 = await this.execCommand(
449:           ["git", "clone", url, "."],
450:           targetDir,
451:           env
452:         );
453: 
454:         if (!result2.success && this.isAuthError(result2.error, credential?.type === "ssh" ? "ssh" : "https")) {
455:           return {
456:             success: false,
457:             output: result2.output,
458:             error: credential?.type === "ssh" 
459:               ? "SSH authentication failed. Please check your private key and repository access."
460:               : "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
461:           };
462:         }
463:         
464:         return {
465:           success: result2.success,
466:           output: result2.output,
467:           error: result2.error || undefined,
468:         };
469:       } finally {
470:         // Clean up temp SSH key file
471:         if (sshKeyPath) {
472:           this.deleteTempSshKeyFile(sshKeyPath);
473:         }
474:       }
475:     } else {
476:       // Clone Fossil repository - inject credentials if HTTPS
477:       let url = repoUrl;
478:       if (credential?.type === "https" && !this.isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
479:         url = this.injectHttpsCredentials(repoUrl, credential);
480:       }
481: 
482:       const result = await this.execCommand(
483:         ["fossil", "clone", url, `${targetDir}/.fossil`],
484:         targetDir
485:       );
486:       
487:       if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, "https")) {
488:         return {
489:           success: false,
490:           output: result.output,
491:           error: "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
492:         };
493:       }
494:       
495:       if (result.success) {
496:         // Open the cloned repo in the target directory
497:         const openResult = await this.openFossil(
498:           `${targetDir}/.fossil`,
499:           targetDir
500:         );
501:         
502:         if (!openResult.success) {
503:           return openResult;
504:         }
505:         
506:         // If sourceBranch specified, checkout that branch
507:         if (sourceBranch) {
508:           const checkoutResult = await this.execCommand(
509:             ["fossil", "checkout", sourceBranch],
510:             targetDir
511:           );
512:           if (!checkoutResult.success) {
513:             return {
514:               success: false,
515:               output: checkoutResult.output,
516:               error: `Failed to checkout source branch '${sourceBranch}': ${checkoutResult.error}`,
517:             };
518:           }
519:         }
520:         
521:         return openResult;
522:       }
523:       
524:       return {
525:         success: false,
526:         output: result.output,
527:         error: result.error || "Failed to clone Fossil repository",
528:       };
529:     }
530:   }
531: 
532:   async importToFossil(
533:     upstreamPath: string,
534:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
535:     fossilPath: string
536:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
537:     if (repoType === "git") {
538:       // Import from Git to Fossil using git fast-export
539:       // fossil import --git creates the repo automatically
540:       
541:       // Use git fast-export piped to fossil import
542:       // We need to run: git fast-export --all | fossil import --git fossilPath
543:       const result = await new Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }>((resolve) => {
544:         const { spawn } = require("child_process");
545:         
546:         const gitExport = spawn("git", ["fast-export", "--all"], { cwd: upstreamPath });
547:         const fossilImport = spawn("fossil", ["import", "--git", fossilPath], { cwd: upstreamPath });
548:         
549:         let stdout = "";
550:         let stderr = "";
551:         
552:         gitExport.stdout.pipe(fossilImport.stdin);
553:         
554:         fossilImport.stdout.on("data", (data) => {
555:           stdout += data.toString();
556:         });
557:         
558:         fossilImport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
559:           stderr += data.toString();
560:         });
561:         
562:         gitExport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
563:           stderr += data.toString();
564:         });
565:         
566:         fossilImport.on("close", (code) => {
567:           resolve({
568:             success: code === 0,
569:             output: stdout,
570:             error: stderr,
571:           });
572:         });
573:         
574:         gitExport.on("error", (err) => {
575:           fossilImport.kill();
576:           resolve({
577:             success: false,
578:             output: "",
579:             error: `Git fast-export failed: ${err.message}`,
580:           });
581:         });
582:       });
583:       
584:       return {
585:         success: result.success,
586:         output: result.output,
587:         error: result.error || undefined,
588:       };
589:     } else {
590:       // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
591:       const result = await this.execCommand(
592:         ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
593:         upstreamPath
594:       );
595:       
596:       return {
597:         success: result.success,
598:         output: result.output,
599:         error: result.error || undefined,
600:       };
601:     }
602:   }
603: 
604:   async openFossilCheckout(
605:     fossilPath: string,
606:     targetPath: string
607:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
608:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
609:     
610:     // Ensure target directory exists
611:     try {
612:       mkdirSync(targetPath, { recursive: true });
613:     } catch {
614:       // Directory might already exist
615:     }
616:     
617:     // Open the fossil repo in the target directory
618:     const result = await this.execCommand(
619:       ["fossil", "open", fossilPath],
620:       targetPath
621:     );
622:     
623:     return {
624:       success: result.success,
625:       output: result.output,
626:       error: result.error || undefined,
627:     };
628:   }
629: 
630:   async exportFromFossil(
631:     fossilPath: string,
632:     upstreamPath: string,
633:     repoType: "git" | "fossil"
634:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
635:     if (repoType === "git") {
636:       // Export from Fossil to Git upstream
637:       // Use fossil export to create a git-fast-export stream
638:       const result = await this.execCommand(
639:         ["fossil", "export", "--git", fossilPath],
640:         upstreamPath
641:       );
642:       
643:       if (result.success) {
644:         // Apply the export to git
645:         const applyResult = await this.execCommand(
646:           ["git", "fast-import"],
647:           upstreamPath
648:         );
649:         return {
650:           success: applyResult.success,
651:           output: applyResult.output,
652:           error: applyResult.error || undefined,
653:         };
654:       }
655:       
656:       return {
657:         success: false,
658:         output: result.output,
659:         error: result.error || undefined,
660:       };
661:     } else {
662:       // For fossil, push directly from checkout
663:       return {
664:         success: true,
665:         output: "Fossil repos sync directly",
666:       };
667:     }
668:   }
669: 
670:   async pushToRemote(
671:     upstreamPath: string,
672:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
673:     credential?: Credential,
674:     branch?: string
675:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
676:     if (repoType === "git") {
677:       let sshKeyPath: string | null = null;
678:       let env: Record<string, string> | undefined = undefined;
679: 
680:       // Handle SSH credentials
681:       if (credential?.type === "ssh") {
682:         sshKeyPath = this.createTempSshKeyFile(credential.privateKey);
683:         env = {
684:           GIT_SSH_COMMAND: this.buildGitSshCommand(sshKeyPath),
685:         };
686:       }
687: 
688:       try {
689:         const pushArgs = branch ? ["push", "origin", branch] : ["push", "origin"];
690:         const result = await this.execCommand(["git", ...pushArgs], upstreamPath, env);
691: 
692:         // Check if the failure is due to no upstream branch configured
693:         // This is expected in test environments or new repos without remotes
694:         if (!result.success && 
695:             (result.error?.includes("no upstream branch") || 
696:              result.error?.includes("has no upstream branch"))) {
697:           return {
698:             success: true,
699:             output: "No remote configured - skipping push",
700:           };
701:         }
702: 
703:         if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, "ssh")) {
704:           return {
705:             success: false,
706:             output: result.output,
707:             error: "SSH authentication failed. Please check your private key and repository access.",
708:           };
709:         }
710: 
711:         return {
712:           success: result.success,
713:           output: result.output,
714:           error: result.error || undefined,
715:         };
716:       } finally {
717:         if (sshKeyPath) {
718:           this.deleteTempSshKeyFile(sshKeyPath);
719:         }
720:       }
721:     } else {
722:       // Fossil push
723:       const args = branch ? ["push", branch] : ["push"];
724:       const result = await this.execCommand(
725:         ["fossil", ...args],
726:         upstreamPath
727:       );
728: 
729:       if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, "https")) {
730:         return {
731:           success: false,
732:           output: result.output,
733:           error: "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
734:         };
735:       }
736: 
737:       return {
738:         success: result.success,
739:         output: result.output,
740:         error: result.error || undefined,
741:       };
742:     }
743:   }
744: 
745:   async setupSessionWorktree(
746:     projectId: string,
747:     sessionId: string,
748:     worktreePath: string
749:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
750:     const { getProjectPath } = await import("../config/paths.js");
751:     const projectPath = getProjectPath(projectId);
752:     const fossilPath = `${projectPath}/repo.fossil`;
753: 
754:     // Ensure worktree directory exists
755:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
756:     try {
757:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
758:     } catch {
759:       // Directory might already exist
760:     }
761: 
762:     // Check if fossil repo exists
763:     const { existsSync } = await import("fs");
764:     if (!existsSync(fossilPath)) {
765:       return {
766:         success: false,
767:         error: "Project fossil repository not found",
768:       };
769:     }
770: 
771:     // Open the fossil repo in the worktree
772:     return await this.openFossil(fossilPath, worktreePath);
773:   }

778:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "up"], agentWorkspacePath);
779:     return {
780:       success: result.success,

786:   async cleanCopyToUpstream(
787:     agentWorkspacePath: string,
788:     upstreamPath: string
789:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
790:     const { readdirSync, statSync, copyFileSync, mkdirSync, unlinkSync, rmdirSync } = await import("fs");
791:     const { join } = await import("path");
792: 
793:     const { existsSync: fsExistsSync } = await import("fs");
794:     
795:     try {
796:       // Get list of files to preserve (VCS directories)
797:       const preserveItems = [".git", ".fossil"];
798:       const itemsToPreserve: string[] = [];
799: 
800:       // Check what exists in upstream that we need to preserve
801:       if (fsExistsSync(upstreamPath)) {
802:         const entries = readdirSync(upstreamPath);
803:         for (const entry of entries) {
804:           if (preserveItems.includes(entry)) {
805:             itemsToPreserve.push(entry);
806:           }
807:         }
808:       }
809: 
810:       // Create a temporary directory to hold preserved items
811:       const { mkdtempSync } = await import("fs");
812:       const { tmpdir } = await import("os");
813:       const tempDir = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), "mimo-preserve-"));
814: 
815:       // Move preserved items to temp (use safeMove for cross-device support)
816:       for (const item of itemsToPreserve) {
817:         const sourcePath = join(upstreamPath, item);
818:         const tempPath = join(tempDir, item);
819:         const isDirectory = statSync(sourcePath).isDirectory();
820:         await this.safeMove(sourcePath, tempPath, isDirectory);
821:       }
822: 
823:       // Delete all remaining items in upstream
824:       const deleteRecursive = (dirPath: string) => {
825:         if (!fsExistsSync(dirPath)) return;
826:         const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
827:         for (const entry of entries) {
828:           const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
829:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
830:             deleteRecursive(fullPath);
831:             rmdirSync(fullPath);
832:           } else {
833:             unlinkSync(fullPath);
834:           }
835:         }
836:       };
837: 
838:       deleteRecursive(upstreamPath);
839: 
840:       // Ensure upstream directory exists
841:       if (!fsExistsSync(upstreamPath)) {
842:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
843:       }
844: 
845:       // Restore preserved items (use safeMove for cross-device support)
846:       for (const item of itemsToPreserve) {
847:         const tempPath = join(tempDir, item);
848:         const destPath = join(upstreamPath, item);
849:         const isDirectory = statSync(tempPath).isDirectory();
850:         await this.safeMove(tempPath, destPath, isDirectory);
851:       }
852: 
853:       // Clean up temp directory
854:       rmdirSync(tempDir);
855: 
856:       // Copy all files from agent-workspace to upstream
857:       const copyRecursive = (source: string, dest: string) => {
858:         if (!fsExistsSync(source)) return;
859: 
860:         const entries = readdirSync(source, { withFileTypes: true });
861:         for (const entry of entries) {
862:           // Skip hidden files and VCS directories
863:           if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) continue;
864: 
865:           const sourcePath = join(source, entry.name);
866:           const destPath = join(dest, entry.name);
867: 
868:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
869:             if (!fsExistsSync(destPath)) {
870:               mkdirSync(destPath, { recursive: true });
871:             }
872:             copyRecursive(sourcePath, destPath);
873:           } else {
874:             copyFileSync(sourcePath, destPath);
875:           }
876:         }
877:       };
878: 
879:       copyRecursive(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath);
880: 
881:       return {
882:         success: true,
883:         output: "Files copied successfully",
884:       };
885:     } catch (error) {
886:       return {
887:         success: false,
888:         error: `Failed to copy files: ${error}`,
889:       };
890:     }
891:   }
892: 
893:   async commitUpstream(
894:     upstreamPath: string,
895:     repoType: "git" | "fossil"
896:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
897:     const message = `Mimo commit at ${new Date().toISOString()}`;
898: 
899:     if (repoType === "git") {
900:       // Git: add all and commit
901:       const addResult = await this.execCommand(["git", "add", "-A"], upstreamPath);
902:       if (!addResult.success) {
903:         return {
904:           success: false,
905:           output: addResult.output,
906:           error: addResult.error || "Failed to stage changes",
907:         };
908:       }
909: 
910:       const commitResult = await this.execCommand(
911:         ["git", "commit", "-m", message],
912:         upstreamPath
913:       );
914: 
915:       // Check if nothing to commit
916:       if (commitResult.error?.includes("nothing to commit") || 
917:           commitResult.output?.includes("nothing to commit")) {
918:         return {
919:           success: true,
920:           output: "No changes to commit",
921:         };
922:       }
923: 
924:       return {
925:         success: commitResult.success,
926:         output: commitResult.output,
927:         error: commitResult.error || undefined,
928:       };
929:     } else {
930:       // Fossil: addremove and commit
931:       const addResult = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "addremove"], upstreamPath);
932:       if (!addResult.success) {
933:         return {
934:           success: false,
935:           output: addResult.output,
936:           error: addResult.error || "Failed to stage changes",
937:         };
938:       }
939: 
940:       const commitResult = await this.execCommand(
941:         ["fossil", "commit", "-m", message],
942:         upstreamPath
943:       );
944: 
945:       return {
946:         success: commitResult.success,
947:         output: commitResult.output,
948:         error: commitResult.error || undefined,
949:       };
950:     }
951:   }
952:

956:     credential?: Credential,

958:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
959:     if (repoType === "git") {

1008:

1010:         return {
1011:           success: false,
1012:           output: result.output,
1013:           error: "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
1014:         };
1015:       }
1016: 
1017:       return {
1018:         success: result.success,
1019:         output: result.output,
1020:         error: result.error || undefined,
1021:       };
```

```
23: // Helper to get authenticated username from cookie
24: async function getAuthUsername(c: Context): Promise<string | null> {
25:   const cookieHeader = c.req.header("Cookie");
26:   const usernameMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/username=([^;]+)/);
27:   const username = usernameMatch ? usernameMatch[1] : null;
28:   if (username) return username;
29:   
30:   // Also check JWT token
31:   const tokenMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/token=([^;]+)/);
32:   const token = tokenMatch ? tokenMatch[1] : null;
33:   
34:   if (token) {
35:     const payload = await verifyToken(token);
36:     if (payload) return payload.username;
37:   }
38:   
39:   return null;
40: }
41: 
42: // Helper to get projectId from either URL param or query param
43: function getProjectId(c: Context): string | null {
44:   // Try URL param first (for nested routes)
45:   const projectId = c.req.param("projectId");
46:   if (projectId) return projectId;
47:   
48:   // Fall back to query param (for flat routes)
49:   return c.req.query("projectId");
50: }
51: 
52: // GET /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - List sessions for a project

100: // POST /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - Create new session
101: router.post("/", async (c: Context) => {
102:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
103:   if (!username) {
104:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
105:   }
106: 
107:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
108:   const name = body.name as string;
109:   const projectId = (body.projectId as string) || getProjectId(c);
110:   const assignedAgentId = (body.assignedAgentId as string) || null;
111: 
112:   if (!name || !projectId) {
113:     return c.text("Name and project ID required", 400);
114:   }
115: 
116:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
117:   if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
118:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
119:   }
120: 
121:   // Create session with upstream and checkout directories
122:   const session = await sessionRepository.create({
123:     name: name as string,
124:     projectId: projectId as string,
125:     owner: username,
126:     assignedAgentId: assignedAgentId || undefined,
127:   });
128: 
129:   // Initialize repository: clone → import to fossil
130:   // Note: checkout is created by agent when it receives session_ready
131:   try {
132:     // Step 1: Clone repository to upstream/
133:     const cloneResult = await vcs.cloneRepository(
134:       project.repoUrl,
135:       project.repoType,
136:       session.upstreamPath,
137:       undefined,
138:       project.sourceBranch
139:     );
140:     
141:     if (!cloneResult.success) {
142:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
143:       return c.text(`Failed to clone repository: ${cloneResult.error}`, 500);
144:     }
145: 
146:     // Step 2: Import to fossil proxy (repo.fossil)
147:     const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
148:     const importResult = await vcs.importToFossil(

150:       project.repoType,

152:     );
153:     
154:     if (!importResult.success) {
155:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
156:       return c.text(`Failed to import to fossil: ${importResult.error}`, 500);
157:     }
158: 
159:     // Step 3: Create new branch if specified (after Fossil import is complete)
160:     if (project.newBranch) {
161:       const branchResult = await vcs.createBranch(
162:         project.newBranch,
163:         project.repoType,
164:         session.upstreamPath
165:       );
166:       if (!branchResult.success) {
167:         await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
168:         return c.text(`Failed to create branch '${project.newBranch}': ${branchResult.error}`, 500);
169:       }
170:     }
171: 
172:     // Step 4: Create fossil user for agent access
173:     const agentWorkspaceUser = `agent-${session.id.slice(0, 8)}`;
174:     const agentWorkspacePassword = crypto.randomUUID().replace(/-/g, "").slice(0, 16);
175:     const userResult = await vcs.createFossilUser(fossilPath, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword);
176:     
177:     if (!userResult.success) {
178:       console.error("[session] Failed to create fossil user:", userResult.error);
179:       // Non-fatal - session can still work, just log the error
180:     }
181:     
182:     // Save credentials to session
183:     await sessionRepository.update(session.id, {
184:       agentWorkspaceUser,
185:       agentWorkspacePassword,
186:     });
187:     
188:     // Step 5: Open fossil checkout in agent-workspace
189:     const openResult = await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
190:     if (!openResult.success) {
191:       console.error("[session] Failed to open fossil in agent-workspace:", openResult.error);
192:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
193:       return c.text("Failed to open fossil checkout", 500);
194:     }
195:   } catch (error) {
196:     console.error("Failed to setup session:", error);
197:     await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
198:     return c.text("Failed to setup session repository", 500);
199:   }
200: 
201:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`);
202: });
203: 
204: // GET /sessions/:id or /projects/:projectId/sessions/:id - View session detail
205: router.get("/:id", async (c: Context) => {
206:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
207:   if (!username) {
208:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
209:   }
210: 
211:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
212:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
213:   
214:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
215:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
216:   }
217: 
218:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(session.projectId);
219:   if (!project) {
220:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
221:   }
222: 
223:   // Get chat history
224:   const chatHistory = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
225:   
226:   // Get assigned agent if any
227:   let agent = undefined;
228:   if (session.assignedAgentId) {
229:     agent = await agentRepository.findById(session.assignedAgentId);
230:   }
231: 
232:   // Get model/mode state from in-memory store
233:   const modelState = sessionStateService.getModelState(sessionId);
234:   const modeState = sessionStateService.getModeState(sessionId);
235: 
236:   // Get fossil port for impact buffer links
237:   const runningServer = fossilServerManager.getRunningServer(sessionId);
238:   const fossilPort = runningServer?.port;
239: 
240:   return c.html(
241:     <SessionDetailPage 
242:       session={session}
243:       project={project}
244:       chatHistory={chatHistory}
245:       agent={agent}
246:       modelState={modelState}
247:       modeState={modeState}
248:       fossilPort={fossilPort}
249:     />
250:   );
251: });
252: 
253: // POST /sessions/:id/cancel - Cancel current ACP request
254: router.post("/:id/cancel", async (c: Context) => {
255:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
256:   if (!username) {
257:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
258:   }
259: 
260:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
261:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
262:   
263:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
264:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
265:   }
266:

268:   
269:   return c.json({ success: cancelled });
270: });

272: // POST /sessions/:id/delete or /projects/:projectId/sessions/:id/delete - Delete session
273: router.post("/:id/delete", async (c: Context) => {
274:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
275:   if (!username) {
276:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
277:   }
278: 
279:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
280:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
281:   
282:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
283:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
284:   }
285: 
286:   // Delete session (agent is independent, not affected)
287:   await sessionRepository.delete(session.projectId, sessionId);
288: 
289:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${session.projectId}/sessions`);
290: });
291: 
292: // GET /sessions/:id/files - Get file tree for a session
293: router.get("/:id/files", async (c: Context) => {
294:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
295:   if (!username) {
296:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
297:   }
298: 
299:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
300:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
301:   
302:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
303:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
304:   }
305: 
306:   // Scan filesystem directly for files
307:   const { readdirSync, statSync } = await import("fs");
308:   const { join, relative } = await import("path");
309:   
310:   const fileTree: { [key: string]: string[] } = {};
311:   
312:   function scanDir(dirPath: string, basePath: string) {
313:     if (!statSync(dirPath, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) {
314:       return;
315:     }
316:     
317:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
318:     
319:     for (const entry of entries) {
320:       const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
321:       const relPath = relative(basePath, fullPath);
322:       
323:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
324:         scanDir(fullPath, basePath);
325:       } else {
326:         const parts = relPath.split("/");
327:         const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
328:         const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
329:         
330:         if (!fileTree[dir]) {
331:           fileTree[dir] = [];
332:         }
333:         fileTree[dir].push(fileName);
334:       }
335:     }
336:   }
337:   
338:   try {
339:     scanDir(session.agentWorkspacePath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
340:   } catch (error) {
341:     console.error("Error scanning checkout:", error);
342:   }
343: 
344:   // Return HTML file tree
345:   let html = `<!DOCTYPE html>
346: <html>
347: <head><title>File Tree</title></head>
348: <body>
349: <div class="file-tree">
350: `;
351: 
352:   for (const [dir, files] of Object.entries(fileTree)) {
353:     html += `  <div class="dir">${dir}/</div>\n`;
354:     for (const file of files) {
355:       html += `    <div class="file">${file}</div>\n`;
356:     }
357:   }
358: 
359:   html += `</div>
360: </body>
361: </html>`;
362: 
363:   return c.html(html);
364: });
365: 
366: // POST /sessions/:id/chat - Save a chat message
367: router.post("/:id/chat", async (c: Context) => {
368:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
369:   if (!username) {
370:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
371:   }
372: 
373:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
374:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
375: 
376:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
377:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
378:   }
379: 
380:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
381:   const message = body.message as string;
382: 
383:   if (!message) {
384:     return c.text("Message required", 400);
385:   }
386: 
387:   await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
388:     role: "user",
389:     content: message,
390:     timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
391:   });
392: 
393:   return c.json({ success: true });
394: });
395: 
396: // GET /sessions/:id/impact - Get real-time impact metrics for a session
397: router.get("/:id/impact", async (c: Context) => {
398:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
399:   if (!username) {
400:     return c.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, 401);
401:   }
402: 
403:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
404:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
405: 
406:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
407:     return c.json({ error: "Session not found" }, 404);
408:   }
409: 
410:   try {
411:     const { impactCalculator } = await import("../impact/calculator.js");
412:     const { getSccService } = await import("../impact/scc-service.js");
413:     const { vcs } = await import("../vcs/index.js");
414: 
415:     // Sync agent-workspace with repo.fossil before calculating impact
416:     const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
417:     const { existsSync } = await import("fs");
418:     const { join } = await import("path");
419:     const fslckoutPath = join(session.agentWorkspacePath, ".fslckout");
420:     
421:     if (existsSync(fossilPath)) {
422:       if (!existsSync(fslckoutPath)) {
423:         // Initialize fossil checkout if not exists
424:         console.log(`[impact] Initializing fossil checkout in agent-workspace...`);
425:         await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
426:       }
427:       // Sync with repo.fossil to get latest changes from agent
428:       console.log(`[impact] Syncing agent-workspace with repo.fossil...`);
429:       await vcs.fossilUp(session.agentWorkspacePath);
430:     }
431: 
432:     // Check if scc is installed - use getter to avoid TDZ issues
433:     const sccService = getSccService();
434:     const sccInstalled = sccService.isInstalled();
435: 
436:     if (!sccInstalled) {
437:       // Return basic file counts without complexity
438:       const { readdirSync, statSync, readFileSync } = await import("fs");
439:       const { join, relative } = await import("path");
440:       const crypto = await import("crypto");
441: 
442:       const scanDir = (dir: string, baseDir: string, files: Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>) => {
443:         if (!statSync(dir, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) return;
444:         const entries = readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true });
445:         for (const entry of entries) {
446:           const fullPath = join(dir, entry.name);
447:           const relPath = relative(baseDir, fullPath);
448:           if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) continue;
449:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
450:             scanDir(fullPath, baseDir, files);
451:           } else {
452:             const stats = statSync(fullPath);
453:             const content = readFileSync(fullPath);
454:             const checksum = crypto.createHash("md5").update(content).digest("hex");
455:             files.set(relPath, { checksum, size: stats.size });
456:           }
457:         }
458:       };
459: 
460:       const upstreamFiles = new Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>();
461:       const workspaceFiles = new Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>();
462: 
463:       scanDir(session.upstreamPath, session.upstreamPath, upstreamFiles);
464:       scanDir(session.agentWorkspacePath, session.agentWorkspacePath, workspaceFiles);
465: 
466:       let newCount = 0, changedCount = 0, deletedCount = 0;
467: 
468:       for (const [path, info] of workspaceFiles) {
469:         if (!upstreamFiles.has(path)) newCount++;
470:         else if (upstreamFiles.get(path)?.checksum !== info.checksum) changedCount++;
471:       }
472: 
473:       for (const [path] of upstreamFiles) {
474:         if (!workspaceFiles.has(path)) deletedCount++;
475:       }
476: 
477:       return c.json({
478:         files: { new: newCount, changed: changedCount, deleted: deletedCount },
479:         sccInstalled: false,
480:         warning: "scc not installed - complexity metrics unavailable",
481:       });
482:     }
483: 
484:     // Calculate full impact with complexity
485:     const result = await impactCalculator.calculateImpact(
486:       sessionId,
487:       session.upstreamPath,
488:       session.agentWorkspacePath
489:     );
490: 
491:     return c.json({
492:       ...result,
493:       sccInstalled: true,
494:     });
495:   } catch (error) {
496:     console.error("[impact] Failed to calculate impact:", error);
497:     return c.json({ error: "Failed to calculate impact" }, 500);
498:   }
499: });
500: 
501: export default router;

(End of file - total 501 lines)
</content>
```

```
39:   );
```

```
63:                   {cred.name} ({cred.type.toUpperCase()})
64:                 </option>
65:               ))}
66:             </select>
67:             <small>Select a credential for private repositories. Type must match URL (HTTPS for https://, SSH for git@).</small>
68:           </div>
```

```
41: projects.post("/", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
42:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
43:   const name = body.name as string;
44:   const repoUrl = body.repoUrl as string;
45:   const repoType = (body.repoType as string) || "git";
46:   const description = body.description as string | undefined;
47:   const credentialId = body.credentialId as string | undefined;

49:   const newBranch = body.newBranch as string | undefined;
50:   const user = c.get("user") as { username: string };
51: 
52:   if (!name || !repoUrl) {
53:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
54:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Name and repository URL are required" />, 400);
55:   }
56: 
57:   // Validate URL format
58:   try {
59:     new URL(repoUrl);
60:   } catch {
61:     // Allow SSH URLs (git@github.com:user/repo.git)
62:     if (!isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
63:       const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
64:       return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Invalid repository URL" />, 400);
65:     }
66:   }
67: 
68:   // Validate repo type
69:   if (repoType !== "git" && repoType !== "fossil") {
70:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
71:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Repository type must be 'git' or 'fossil'" />, 400);
72:   }
73: 
74:   // Validate description length
75:   if (description && description.length > 500) {
76:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
77:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Description must be 500 characters or less" />, 400);
78:   }
79:

81:   if (credentialId) {
82:     const credential = await credentialRepository.findById(credentialId, user.username);
83:     if (!credential) {
84:       const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
85:       return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Selected credential not found" />, 400);
86:     }
87:     
88:     // Validate credential type matches URL type
89:     const expectedType = getCredentialTypeFromUrl(repoUrl);
90:     if (credential.type !== expectedType) {

92:       return c.html(
93:         <ProjectCreatePage 
94:           credentials={credentials} 
95:           error={`Credential type does not match repository URL type. Expected ${expectedType.toUpperCase()} but got ${credential.type.toUpperCase()}`} 
96:         />, 
97:         400
98:       );
99:     }
100:   }
101:

103:     const project = await projectRepository.create({
104:       name,
105:       repoUrl,
106:       repoType: repoType as "git" | "fossil",

108:       description: description || undefined,
109:       credentialId: credentialId || undefined,
110:       sourceBranch: sourceBranch || undefined,
111:       newBranch: newBranch || undefined,
112:     });
113: 
114:     return c.redirect(`/projects/${project.id}`, 302);
115:   } catch (error) {
116:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
117:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Failed to create project" />, 500);
118:   }
119: });

290:

295:       name: impact.sessionName,
296:       exists: !!session,
297:     });
298:   }
```

```
267:       }, 10000);

275:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
276:

280:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "oldfile.txt"), "old content");

284:

286:

293:         const vcs = new VCS();
294:         const agentWorkspacePath = join(testHome, "agent-workspace-crossdev");
295:         const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "upstream-crossdev");
296:         
297:         mkdirSync(agentWorkspacePath, { recursive: true });
298:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
299:         mkdirSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git"), { recursive: true });
300:         
301:         // Create a file in .git that should be preserved
302:         const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
303:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "config"), "[core] repositoryformatversion = 0");
304:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "newfile.txt"), "new content");
305:         
306:         // The safeMove should handle cross-device scenarios by falling back to copy+delete
307:         const result = await vcs.cleanCopyToUpstream(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath);
308:         
309:         expect(result.success).toBe(true);
310:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "config"))).toBe(true);

314:       it("should preserve complete .git structure including objects directory", async () => {
315:         const vcs = new VCS();
316:         const agentWorkspacePath = join(testHome, "agent-workspace-git-complete");
317:         const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "upstream-git-complete");
318:         
319:         mkdirSync(agentWorkspacePath, { recursive: true });
320:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
321:         
322:         // Create complete .git structure
323:         const gitPath = join(upstreamPath, ".git");
324:         mkdirSync(gitPath, { recursive: true });
325:         mkdirSync(join(gitPath, "objects"), { recursive: true });
326:         mkdirSync(join(gitPath, "objects", "pack"), { recursive: true });
327:         mkdirSync(join(gitPath, "refs", "heads"), { recursive: true });
328:         mkdirSync(join(gitPath, "refs", "tags"), { recursive: true });
329:         
330:         const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
331:         writeFileSync(join(gitPath, "config"), "[core] repositoryformatversion = 0");
332:         writeFileSync(join(gitPath, "HEAD"), "ref: refs/heads/main");
333:         writeFileSync(join(gitPath, "packed-refs"), "# packed-refs");
334:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "README.md"), "# Test");
335:         
336:         const result = await vcs.cleanCopyToUpstream(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath);
337:         
338:         expect(result.success).toBe(true);
339:         // Verify all critical .git directories exist
340:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git"))).toBe(true);
341:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "objects"))).toBe(true);
342:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "objects", "pack"))).toBe(true);
343:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "refs"))).toBe(true);
344:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "refs", "heads"))).toBe(true);
345:         // Verify files are preserved
346:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "config"))).toBe(true);
347:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "HEAD"))).toBe(true);
348:         // Verify agent files are copied
349:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "README.md"))).toBe(true);
350:       }, 10000);

379:       it("should preserve file timestamps during copy", async () => {
380:         const vcs = new VCS();
381:         const agentWorkspacePath = join(testHome, "agent-workspace-timestamps");
382:         const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "upstream-timestamps");
383:         
384:         mkdirSync(agentWorkspacePath, { recursive: true });
385:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
386:         mkdirSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git"), { recursive: true });
387:         
388:         const { writeFileSync, statSync } = await import("fs");
389:         const gitConfigPath = join(upstreamPath, ".git", "config");
390:         writeFileSync(gitConfigPath, "config content");
391:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "file.txt"), "content");
392:         
393:         // Get original timestamp
394:         const originalStat = statSync(gitConfigPath);
395:         const originalMtime = originalStat.mtime;
396:         
397:         // Wait a bit to ensure timestamp would change if not preserved
398:         await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
399:         
400:         const result = await vcs.cleanCopyToUpstream(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath);
401:         
402:         expect(result.success).toBe(true);
403:         
404:         // Verify timestamp was preserved
405:         const newStat = statSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "config"));
406:         expect(newStat.mtime.getTime()).toBe(originalMtime.getTime());
407:       }, 10000);
408: 
409:       it("should handle git repository end-to-end", async () => {
410:         const vcs = new VCS();
411:         const { execSync, execFileSync } = await import("child_process");
412:         const agentWorkspacePath = join(testHome, "agent-workspace-e2e");
413:         const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "upstream-e2e");
414:         
415:         // Setup agent workspace
416:         mkdirSync(agentWorkspacePath, { recursive: true });
417:         const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
418:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "new-feature.txt"), "New feature content");
419:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "README.md"), "Updated README");
420:         
421:         // Setup upstream as proper git repo
422:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
423:         execSync("git init", { cwd: upstreamPath });
424:         execSync("git config user.email \"test@test.com\"", { cwd: upstreamPath });
425:         execSync("git config user.name \"Test User\"", { cwd: upstreamPath });
426:         execFileSync("git", ["commit", "--allow-empty", "-m", "Initial commit"], { cwd: upstreamPath });
427:         
428:         // Create initial file
429:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "existing.txt"), "Existing content");
430:         execSync("git add -A", { cwd: upstreamPath });
431:         execSync("git commit -m \"Add existing file\"", { cwd: upstreamPath });
432:         
433:         const result = await vcs.cleanCopyToUpstream(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath);
434:         
435:         expect(result.success).toBe(true);
436:         // Verify .git is preserved and functional
437:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git"))).toBe(true);
438:         // Verify new files from agent are present
439:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "new-feature.txt"))).toBe(true);
440:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "README.md"))).toBe(true);
441:         // Verify old files are removed
442:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "existing.txt"))).toBe(false);
443:         
444:         // Verify git still works
445:         const gitStatus = execSync("git status --porcelain", { cwd: upstreamPath, encoding: "utf8" });
446:         expect(gitStatus).toContain("new-feature.txt");
447:         expect(gitStatus).toContain("README.md");
448:       }, 15000);

450:       it("should handle nested directory structures", async () => {
451:         const vcs = new VCS();
452:         const agentWorkspacePath = join(testHome, "agent-workspace-nested");
453:         const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "upstream-nested");
454:         
455:         mkdirSync(agentWorkspacePath, { recursive: true });
456:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
457:         mkdirSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git"), { recursive: true });
458:         
459:         // Create nested structure in agent workspace
460:         mkdirSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "src", "components"), { recursive: true });
461:         mkdirSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "src", "utils"), { recursive: true });
462:         
463:         const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
464:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "src", "components", "Button.tsx"), "export const Button = () => {}");
465:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "src", "utils", "helpers.ts"), "export const helper = () => {}");
466:         writeFileSync(join(agentWorkspacePath, "package.json"), "{}");
467:         
468:         // Create old files in upstream that should be removed
469:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "config"), "git config");
470:         mkdirSync(join(upstreamPath, "old"), { recursive: true });
471:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "old", "legacy.js"), "old code");
472:         
473:         const result = await vcs.cleanCopyToUpstream(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath);
474:         
475:         expect(result.success).toBe(true);
476:         // Verify nested structure is preserved
477:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "src", "components", "Button.tsx"))).toBe(true);
478:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "src", "utils", "helpers.ts"))).toBe(true);
479:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "package.json"))).toBe(true);
480:         // Verify .git is preserved
481:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git", "config"))).toBe(true);
482:         // Verify old files are removed
483:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "old", "legacy.js"))).toBe(false);
484:         expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, "old"))).toBe(false);
485:       }, 10000);

615:   describe("Branch Operations", () => {
616:     describe("createBranch", () => {
617:       it("should create a new branch in Git repository", async () => {
618:         const vcs = new VCS();
619:         const { execSync } = await import("child_process");
620:         const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "git-branch-test");
621:         
622:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
623:         execSync("git init", { cwd: upstreamPath });
624:         execSync("git config user.email \"test@test.com\"", { cwd: upstreamPath });
625:         execSync("git config user.name \"Test User\"", { cwd: upstreamPath });
626:         
627:         const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
628:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "test.txt"), "test");
629:         execSync("git add .", { cwd: upstreamPath });
630:         execSync('git commit -m "Initial"', { cwd: upstreamPath });
631:         
632:         const result = await vcs.createBranch("feature-branch", "git", upstreamPath);
633:         
634:         expect(result.success).toBe(true);
635:         
636:         // Verify branch was created
637:         const branchOutput = execSync("git branch", { cwd: upstreamPath, encoding: "utf8" });
638:         expect(branchOutput).toContain("feature-branch");
639:         
640:         // Verify we're on the new branch
641:         const currentBranch = execSync("git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD", { cwd: upstreamPath, encoding: "utf8" });
642:         expect(currentBranch.trim()).toBe("feature-branch");
643:       }, 15000);
644: 
645:       it("should overwrite existing Git branch with -B flag", async () => {
646:         const vcs = new VCS();
647:         const { execSync } = await import("child_process");
648:         const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "git-branch-overwrite-test");
649:         
650:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
651:         execSync("git init", { cwd: upstreamPath });
652:         execSync("git config user.email \"test@test.com\"", { cwd: upstreamPath });
653:         execSync("git config user.name \"Test User\"", { cwd: upstreamPath });
654:         
655:         const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
656:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "test.txt"), "test");
657:         execSync("git add .", { cwd: upstreamPath });
658:         execSync('git commit -m "Initial"', { cwd: upstreamPath });
659:         
660:         // Create initial branch
661:         await vcs.createBranch("existing-branch", "git", upstreamPath);
662:         
663:         // Make a commit on master
664:         execSync("git checkout master", { cwd: upstreamPath });
665:         writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "another.txt"), "another");
666:         execSync("git add .", { cwd: upstreamPath });
667:         execSync('git commit -m "Another commit"', { cwd: upstreamPath });
668:         
669:         // Try to create branch that already exists - should overwrite
670:         const result = await vcs.createBranch("existing-branch", "git", upstreamPath);
671:         
672:         expect(result.success).toBe(true);
673:         
674:         // Verify we're on the new branch
675:         const currentBranch = execSync("git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD", { cwd: upstreamPath, encoding: "utf8" });
676:         expect(currentBranch.trim()).toBe("existing-branch");
677:       }, 15000);
```
