385:   async cloneRepository(
386:     repoUrl: string,
387:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
388:     targetDir: string,
389:     credential?: Credential,
390:     sourceBranch?: string
391:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
392:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
393:     
394:     // Ensure target directory exists
395:     try {
396:       mkdirSync(targetDir, { recursive: true });
397:     } catch {
398:       // Directory might already exist
399:     }
400: 
401:     if (repoType === "git") {
402:       let url = repoUrl;
403:       let sshKeyPath: string | null = null;
404:       let env: Record<string, string> | undefined = undefined;
405: 
406:       // Handle credentials
407:       if (credential) {
408:         if (credential.type === "https" && !this.isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
409:           url = this.injectHttpsCredentials(repoUrl, credential);
410:         } else if (credential.type === "ssh" && this.isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
411:           // Create temp SSH key file
412:           sshKeyPath = this.createTempSshKeyFile(credential.privateKey);
413:           env = {
414:             GIT_SSH_COMMAND: this.buildGitSshCommand(sshKeyPath),
415:           };
416:         }
417:       }
418: 
419:       try {
420:         // Clone Git repository with optional branch
421:         const cloneArgs = sourceBranch 
422:           ? ["git", "clone", "--branch", sourceBranch, url, targetDir]
423:           : ["git", "clone", url, targetDir];
424:         const result = await this.execCommand(
425:           cloneArgs,
426:           targetDir,
427:           env
428:         );
429:         
430:         if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, credential?.type === "ssh" ? "ssh" : "https")) {
431:           return {
432:             success: false,
433:             output: result.output,
434:             error: credential?.type === "ssh" 
435:               ? "SSH authentication failed. Please check your private key and repository access."
436:               : "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
437:           };
438:         }
439:         
440:         if (result.success) {
441:           return {
442:             success: true,
443:             output: result.output,
444:           };
445:         }
446:         
447:         // If git clone failed but directory has content, try cloning into current directory
448:         const result2 = await this.execCommand(
449:           ["git", "clone", url, "."],
450:           targetDir,
451:           env
452:         );
453: 
454:         if (!result2.success && this.isAuthError(result2.error, credential?.type === "ssh" ? "ssh" : "https")) {
455:           return {
456:             success: false,
457:             output: result2.output,
458:             error: credential?.type === "ssh" 
459:               ? "SSH authentication failed. Please check your private key and repository access."
460:               : "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
461:           };
462:         }
463:         
464:         return {
465:           success: result2.success,
466:           output: result2.output,
467:           error: result2.error || undefined,
468:         };
469:       } finally {
470:         // Clean up temp SSH key file
471:         if (sshKeyPath) {
472:           this.deleteTempSshKeyFile(sshKeyPath);
473:         }
474:       }
475:     } else {
476:       // Clone Fossil repository - inject credentials if HTTPS
477:       let url = repoUrl;
478:       if (credential?.type === "https" && !this.isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
479:         url = this.injectHttpsCredentials(repoUrl, credential);
480:       }
481: 
482:       const result = await this.execCommand(
483:         ["fossil", "clone", url, `${targetDir}/.fossil`],
484:         targetDir
485:       );
486:       
487:       if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, "https")) {
488:         return {
489:           success: false,
490:           output: result.output,
491:           error: "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
492:         };
493:       }
494:       
495:       if (result.success) {
496:         // Open the cloned repo in the target directory
497:         const openResult = await this.openFossil(
498:           `${targetDir}/.fossil`,
499:           targetDir
500:         );
501:         
502:         if (!openResult.success) {
503:           return openResult;
504:         }
505:         
506:         // If sourceBranch specified, checkout that branch
507:         if (sourceBranch) {
508:           const checkoutResult = await this.execCommand(
509:             ["fossil", "checkout", sourceBranch],
510:             targetDir
511:           );
512:           if (!checkoutResult.success) {
513:             return {
514:               success: false,
515:               output: checkoutResult.output,
516:               error: `Failed to checkout source branch '${sourceBranch}': ${checkoutResult.error}`,
517:             };
518:           }
519:         }
520:         
521:         return openResult;
522:       }
523:       
524:       return {
525:         success: false,
526:         output: result.output,
527:         error: result.error || "Failed to clone Fossil repository",
528:       };
529:     }
530:   }
531: 
532:   async importToFossil(
533:     upstreamPath: string,
534:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
535:     fossilPath: string
536:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
537:     if (repoType === "git") {
538:       // Import from Git to Fossil using git fast-export
539:       // fossil import --git creates the repo automatically
540:       
541:       // Use git fast-export piped to fossil import
542:       // We need to run: git fast-export --all | fossil import --git fossilPath
543:       const result = await new Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }>((resolve) => {
544:         const { spawn } = require("child_process");
545:         
546:         const gitExport = spawn("git", ["fast-export", "--all"], { cwd: upstreamPath });
547:         const fossilImport = spawn("fossil", ["import", "--git", fossilPath], { cwd: upstreamPath });
548:         
549:         let stdout = "";
550:         let stderr = "";
551:         
552:         gitExport.stdout.pipe(fossilImport.stdin);
553:         
554:         fossilImport.stdout.on("data", (data) => {
555:           stdout += data.toString();
556:         });
557:         
558:         fossilImport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
559:           stderr += data.toString();
560:         });
561:         
562:         gitExport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
563:           stderr += data.toString();
564:         });
565:         
566:         fossilImport.on("close", (code) => {
567:           resolve({
568:             success: code === 0,
569:             output: stdout,
570:             error: stderr,
571:           });
572:         });
573:         
574:         gitExport.on("error", (err) => {
575:           fossilImport.kill();
576:           resolve({
577:             success: false,
578:             output: "",
579:             error: `Git fast-export failed: ${err.message}`,
580:           });
581:         });
582:       });
583:       
584:       return {
585:         success: result.success,
586:         output: result.output,
587:         error: result.error || undefined,
588:       };
589:     } else {
590:       // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
591:       const result = await this.execCommand(
592:         ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
593:         upstreamPath
594:       );
595:       
596:       return {
597:         success: result.success,
598:         output: result.output,
599:         error: result.error || undefined,
600:       };
601:     }
602:   }
603: 
604:   async openFossilCheckout(
605:     fossilPath: string,
606:     targetPath: string
607:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
608:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
609:     
610:     // Ensure target directory exists
611:     try {
612:       mkdirSync(targetPath, { recursive: true });
613:     } catch {
614:       // Directory might already exist
615:     }
616:     
617:     // Open the fossil repo in the target directory
618:     const result = await this.execCommand(
619:       ["fossil", "open", fossilPath],
620:       targetPath
621:     );
622:     
623:     return {
624:       success: result.success,
625:       output: result.output,
626:       error: result.error || undefined,
627:     };
628:   }
629: 
630:   async exportFromFossil(
631:     fossilPath: string,
632:     upstreamPath: string,
633:     repoType: "git" | "fossil"
634:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
635:     if (repoType === "git") {
636:       // Export from Fossil to Git upstream
637:       // Use fossil export to create a git-fast-export stream
638:       const result = await this.execCommand(
639:         ["fossil", "export", "--git", fossilPath],
640:         upstreamPath
641:       );
642:       
643:       if (result.success) {
644:         // Apply the export to git
645:         const applyResult = await this.execCommand(
646:           ["git", "fast-import"],
647:           upstreamPath
648:         );
649:         return {
650:           success: applyResult.success,
651:           output: applyResult.output,
652:           error: applyResult.error || undefined,
653:         };
654:       }
655:       
656:       return {
657:         success: false,
658:         output: result.output,
659:         error: result.error || undefined,
660:       };
661:     } else {
662:       // For fossil, push directly from checkout
663:       return {
664:         success: true,
665:         output: "Fossil repos sync directly",
666:       };
667:     }
668:   }
669: 
670:   async pushToRemote(
671:     upstreamPath: string,
672:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
673:     credential?: Credential,
674:     branch?: string
675:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
676:     if (repoType === "git") {
677:       let sshKeyPath: string | null = null;
678:       let env: Record<string, string> | undefined = undefined;
679: 
680:       // Handle SSH credentials
681:       if (credential?.type === "ssh") {
682:         sshKeyPath = this.createTempSshKeyFile(credential.privateKey);
683:         env = {
684:           GIT_SSH_COMMAND: this.buildGitSshCommand(sshKeyPath),
685:         };
686:       }
687: 
688:       try {
689:         const pushArgs = branch ? ["push", "origin", branch] : ["push", "origin"];
690:         const result = await this.execCommand(["git", ...pushArgs], upstreamPath, env);
691: 
692:         // Check if the failure is due to no upstream branch configured
693:         // This is expected in test environments or new repos without remotes
694:         if (!result.success && 
695:             (result.error?.includes("no upstream branch") || 
696:              result.error?.includes("has no upstream branch"))) {
697:           return {
698:             success: true,
699:             output: "No remote configured - skipping push",
700:           };
701:         }
702: 
703:         if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, "ssh")) {
704:           return {
705:             success: false,
706:             output: result.output,
707:             error: "SSH authentication failed. Please check your private key and repository access.",
708:           };
709:         }
710: 
711:         return {
712:           success: result.success,
713:           output: result.output,
714:           error: result.error || undefined,
715:         };
716:       } finally {
717:         if (sshKeyPath) {
718:           this.deleteTempSshKeyFile(sshKeyPath);
719:         }
720:       }
721:     } else {
722:       // Fossil push
723:       const args = branch ? ["push", branch] : ["push"];
724:       const result = await this.execCommand(
725:         ["fossil", ...args],
726:         upstreamPath
727:       );
728: 
729:       if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, "https")) {
730:         return {
731:           success: false,
732:           output: result.output,
733:           error: "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
734:         };
735:       }
736: 
737:       return {
738:         success: result.success,
739:         output: result.output,
740:         error: result.error || undefined,
741:       };
742:     }
743:   }
744: 
745:   async setupSessionWorktree(
746:     projectId: string,
747:     sessionId: string,
748:     worktreePath: string
749:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
750:     const { getProjectPath } = await import("../config/paths.js");
751:     const projectPath = getProjectPath(projectId);
752:     const fossilPath = `${projectPath}/repo.fossil`;
753: 
754:     // Ensure worktree directory exists
755:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
756:     try {
757:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
758:     } catch {
759:       // Directory might already exist
760:     }
761: 
762:     // Check if fossil repo exists
763:     const { existsSync } = await import("fs");
764:     if (!existsSync(fossilPath)) {
765:       return {
766:         success: false,
767:         error: "Project fossil repository not found",
768:       };
769:     }
770: 
771:     // Open the fossil repo in the worktree
772:     return await this.openFossil(fossilPath, worktreePath);
773:   }
774: 
775:   // New methods for commit flow
776: 
777:   async fossilUp(agentWorkspacePath: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
778:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "up"], agentWorkspacePath);
779:     return {
780:       success: result.success,
781:       output: result.output,
782:       error: result.error || undefined,
783:     };
784:   }
785: 
786:   async cleanCopyToUpstream(
787:     agentWorkspacePath: string,
788:     upstreamPath: string
789:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
790:     const { readdirSync, statSync, copyFileSync, mkdirSync, unlinkSync, rmdirSync } = await import("fs");
791:     const { join } = await import("path");
792: 
793:     const { existsSync: fsExistsSync } = await import("fs");
794:     
795:     try {
796:       // Get list of files to preserve (VCS directories)
797:       const preserveItems = [".git", ".fossil"];
798:       const itemsToPreserve: string[] = [];
799: 
800:       // Check what exists in upstream that we need to preserve
801:       if (fsExistsSync(upstreamPath)) {
802:         const entries = readdirSync(upstreamPath);
803:         for (const entry of entries) {
804:           if (preserveItems.includes(entry)) {
805:             itemsToPreserve.push(entry);
806:           }
807:         }
808:       }
809: 
810:       // Create a temporary directory to hold preserved items
811:       const { mkdtempSync } = await import("fs");
812:       const { tmpdir } = await import("os");
813:       const tempDir = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), "mimo-preserve-"));
814: 
815:       // Move preserved items to temp (use safeMove for cross-device support)
816:       for (const item of itemsToPreserve) {
817:         const sourcePath = join(upstreamPath, item);
818:         const tempPath = join(tempDir, item);
819:         const isDirectory = statSync(sourcePath).isDirectory();
820:         await this.safeMove(sourcePath, tempPath, isDirectory);
821:       }
822: 
823:       // Delete all remaining items in upstream
824:       const deleteRecursive = (dirPath: string) => {
825:         if (!fsExistsSync(dirPath)) return;
826:         const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
827:         for (const entry of entries) {
828:           const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
829:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
830:             deleteRecursive(fullPath);
831:             rmdirSync(fullPath);
832:           } else {
833:             unlinkSync(fullPath);
834:           }
835:         }
836:       };
837: 
838:       deleteRecursive(upstreamPath);
839: 
840:       // Ensure upstream directory exists
841:       if (!fsExistsSync(upstreamPath)) {
842:         mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
843:       }
844: 
845:       // Restore preserved items (use safeMove for cross-device support)
846:       for (const item of itemsToPreserve) {
847:         const tempPath = join(tempDir, item);
848:         const destPath = join(upstreamPath, item);
849:         const isDirectory = statSync(tempPath).isDirectory();
850:         await this.safeMove(tempPath, destPath, isDirectory);
851:       }
852: 
853:       // Clean up temp directory
854:       rmdirSync(tempDir);
855: 
856:       // Copy all files from agent-workspace to upstream
857:       const copyRecursive = (source: string, dest: string) => {
858:         if (!fsExistsSync(source)) return;
859: 
860:         const entries = readdirSync(source, { withFileTypes: true });
861:         for (const entry of entries) {
862:           // Skip hidden files and VCS directories
863:           if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) continue;
864: 
865:           const sourcePath = join(source, entry.name);
866:           const destPath = join(dest, entry.name);
867: 
868:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
869:             if (!fsExistsSync(destPath)) {
870:               mkdirSync(destPath, { recursive: true });
871:             }
872:             copyRecursive(sourcePath, destPath);
873:           } else {
874:             copyFileSync(sourcePath, destPath);
875:           }
876:         }
877:       };
878: 
879:       copyRecursive(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath);
880: 
881:       return {
882:         success: true,
883:         output: "Files copied successfully",
884:       };
885:     } catch (error) {
886:       return {
887:         success: false,
888:         error: `Failed to copy files: ${error}`,
889:       };
890:     }
891:   }
892: 
893:   async commitUpstream(
894:     upstreamPath: string,
895:     repoType: "git" | "fossil"
896:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
897:     const message = `Mimo commit at ${new Date().toISOString()}`;
898: 
899:     if (repoType === "git") {
900:       // Git: add all and commit
901:       const addResult = await this.execCommand(["git", "add", "-A"], upstreamPath);
902:       if (!addResult.success) {
903:         return {
904:           success: false,
905:           output: addResult.output,
906:           error: addResult.error || "Failed to stage changes",
907:         };
908:       }
909: 
910:       const commitResult = await this.execCommand(
911:         ["git", "commit", "-m", message],
912:         upstreamPath
913:       );
914: 
915:       // Check if nothing to commit
916:       if (commitResult.error?.includes("nothing to commit") || 
917:           commitResult.output?.includes("nothing to commit")) {
918:         return {
919:           success: true,
920:           output: "No changes to commit",
921:         };
922:       }
923: 
924:       return {
925:         success: commitResult.success,
926:         output: commitResult.output,
927:         error: commitResult.error || undefined,
928:       };
929:     } else {
930:       // Fossil: addremove and commit
931:       const addResult = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "addremove"], upstreamPath);
932:       if (!addResult.success) {
933:         return {
934:           success: false,
935:           output: addResult.output,
936:           error: addResult.error || "Failed to stage changes",
937:         };
938:       }
939: 
940:       const commitResult = await this.execCommand(
941:         ["fossil", "commit", "-m", message],
942:         upstreamPath
943:       );
944: 
945:       return {
946:         success: commitResult.success,
947:         output: commitResult.output,
948:         error: commitResult.error || undefined,
949:       };
950:     }
951:   }
952: 
953:   async pushUpstream(
954:     upstreamPath: string,
955:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
956:     credential?: Credential,
957:     branch?: string
958:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
959:     if (repoType === "git") {
960:       let sshKeyPath: string | null = null;
961:       let env: Record<string, string> | undefined = undefined;
962: 
963:       // Handle SSH credentials
964:       if (credential?.type === "ssh") {
965:         sshKeyPath = this.createTempSshKeyFile(credential.privateKey);
966:         env = {
967:           GIT_SSH_COMMAND: this.buildGitSshCommand(sshKeyPath),
968:         };
969:       }
970: 
971:       try {
972:         const pushArgs = branch ? ["push", "origin", branch] : ["push", "origin"];
973:         const result = await this.execCommand(["git", ...pushArgs], upstreamPath, env);
974: 
975:         // Check if the failure is due to no upstream branch configured
976:         // This is expected in test environments or new repos without remotes
977:         if (!result.success && 
978:             (result.error?.includes("no upstream branch") || 
979:              result.error?.includes("has no upstream branch"))) {
980:           return {
981:             success: true,
982:             output: "No remote configured - skipping push",
983:           };
984:         }
985: 
986:         if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, credential?.type === "ssh" ? "ssh" : "https")) {
987:           return {
988:             success: false,
989:             output: result.output,
990:             error: credential?.type === "ssh" 
991:               ? "SSH authentication failed. Please check your private key and repository access."
992:               : "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
993:           };
994:         }
995: 
996:         return {
997:           success: result.success,
998:           output: result.output,
999:           error: result.error || undefined,
1000:         };
1001:       } finally {
1002:         if (sshKeyPath) {
1003:           this.deleteTempSshKeyFile(sshKeyPath);
1004:         }
1005:       }
1006:     } else {
1007:       const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "push"], upstreamPath);
1008: 
1009:       if (!result.success && this.isAuthError(result.error, "https")) {
1010:         return {
1011:           success: false,
1012:           output: result.output,
1013:           error: "Authentication failed. Please check your credentials and repository access.",
1014:         };
1015:       }
1016: 
1017:       return {
1018:         success: result.success,
1019:         output: result.output,
1020:         error: result.error || undefined,
1021:       };
1022:     }

69:     if (input.description && input.description.length > 500) {
70:       throw new Error("Description must be 500 characters or less");
71:     }
72:

75:     
76:     if (!existsSync(projectPath)) {
77:       mkdirSync(projectPath, { recursive: true });

95:       dump(projectData),

102:     };

108:       return null;
